      <span class="title">

        <%= name === "hold-bin" ? '<svg viewBox="0 0 200 200" class="cart-menu-holdbin-icon"><use xlink:href="/static/a80a50dad305e98f897ec936997e6b17.svg#icon-holdbin"></use></svg>' : "" %>
        <%= hasItem ? "<svg viewBox=\"0 0 200 200\" class=\"cart-menu-in-cart-icon\"><use xlink:href=\"/static/a80a50dad305e98f897ec936997e6b17.svg#icon-in-cart\"></use></svg>" : "" %>
        <%- displayName %></span>

    <%= (header || cartHeader) ? "</a>" : "" %>
